21/12/23, 14:20 - Gagan C Nitk: Greetings NITK Surathkal students !
 
We're happy to open applications for the *Finlatics Financial Markets Experience Program*, an online *live project* that helps students *gain work experience* in *Equity Markets* at the *National Institute of Technology Karnataka (NITK) Surathkal*. 

*No prior domain knowledge* is required to be a part of the project as it includes personalized *mentoring*, guidance and *live sessions* to train students. The project runs at leading institutes including *IIT Bombay*, *IIT Delhi*, *IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Benefits* Post-Completion:
1. *Certificate of Work Experience*
2. *Letter of Recommendation*.

To apply, please use the link below:

https://www.finlatics.com/smscampain/application/index.php?utm_src=nitkw

Please note that you can take a *break* on the program in case you need it for any *exams*, *assignments* or *personal commitments*.

*Project Duration* : 2 months

*Project start*: Flexible on student choice. To *balance* it along with exams or assignments, students can choose to start it once they are completed. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee:  Rs. 1999 + GST / Rs. 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*: A *25-30% Fee Waiver* shall be given to all *National Institute of Technology Karnataka (NITK) Surathkal* students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1499 + GST / Rs. 2049 + GST.

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

*No payment* has to be made right now

*Incentives* : upto Rs. 6000 (for top performers) 

The *application* process would take *2-3 mins* of your time. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics
